\"The Envoy codebase implements dynamic cluster discovery and health checking through several key components:\\n\\n**CDS (Cluster Discovery Service) Subscription**: The core CDS implementation resides in source/common/upstream/cds_api_impl.cc/h, which handles subscription to cluster discovery service. Additional CDS-related files include source/common/upstream/cds_api_helper.cc/h for helper utilities, source/common/upstream/cluster_discovery_manager.cc/h for managing cluster discovery, and source/common/upstream/od_cds_api_impl.cc/h for On-Demand CDS implementation.\\n\\n**Cluster Manager & Update Logic**: The cluster manager update logic is implemented in source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc/h, which is the central component coordinating cluster lifecycle. Supporting files include source/common/upstream/cluster_factory_impl.cc/h for cluster instantiation, source/common/upstream/cluster_update_tracker.cc/h for tracking updates, and source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc/h for core upstream functionality.\\n\\n**Active Health Checking**: The active health check infrastructure is built on source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.cc/h in the common layer. Protocol-specific health checker implementations are in source/extensions/health_checkers/: grpc/, http/, tcp/, redis/, and thrift/ subdirectories. Health check event logging is handled by source/common/upstream/health_checker_event_logger.cc/h. Health discovery service is implemented in source/common/upstream/health_discovery_service.cc/h. The scheduler integration for health checks is present in the base health checker implementation and scheduler classes in source/common/upstream/edf_scheduler.h and source/common/upstream/wrsq_scheduler.h.\\n\\n**Outlier Detection Integration**: Outlier detection is implemented in source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.cc/h, which integrates with the health checking and load balancing systems to handle host ejection based on abnormal behavior.\\n\\n**xDS Subscription & Configuration Management**: The gRPC subscription infrastructure for receiving cluster configuration updates is in source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/: grpc_subscription_impl.cc/h, grpc_mux_impl.cc/h, new_grpc_mux_impl.cc/h for multiplexed subscriptions, delta_subscription_state.cc/h for delta subscription logic, and xds_mux/ subdirectory for XDS-specific mux implementations. Supporting components include watch_map.cc/h for resource tracking, pausable_ack_queue.cc/h for ACK handling, and eds_resources_cache_impl.cc/h for endpoint resource caching.\\n\\n**Cluster Implementations**: Various cluster types that integrate with discovery include source/extensions/clusters/eds/ for endpoint discovery service clusters, source/extensions/clusters/aggregate/ for aggregated clusters, and source/extensions/clusters/ subdirectories for other cluster types like logical_dns, strict_dns, static, original_dst, and dynamic_forward_proxy.\\n\\n**Load Balancing Integration**: Load balancing policies in source/extensions/load_balancing_policies/ integrate with cluster health information and outlier detection. Key implementations include load_balancer_impl.cc/h and thread_aware_lb_impl.cc/h for the common framework, plus specific policies in round_robin/, least_request/, ring_hash/, maglev/, subset/, and random/ subdirectories.\\n\\n**Monitoring & Statistics**: Load statistics reporting for LDS (Load Distribution Service) is in source/common/upstream/load_stats_reporter.cc/h. Host utility functions for managing endpoint information are in source/common/upstream/host_utility.cc/h.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":975,"cache_read_input_tokens":41216,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":975},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"42b24306-213b-41de-8bf2-cf7388766a20","uuid":"74c1550a-7639-4180-a433-5e249b2570c6"}

\"The Envoy codebase implements dynamic cluster discovery and health checking through several key components:\\n\\n**CDS (Cluster Discovery Service) Subscription**: The core CDS implementation resides in source/common/upstream/cds_api_impl.cc/h, which handles subscription to cluster discovery service. Additional CDS-related files include source/common/upstream/cds_api_helper.cc/h for helper utilities, source/common/upstream/cluster_discovery_manager.cc/h for managing cluster discovery, and source/common/upstream/od_cds_api_impl.cc/h for On-Demand CDS implementation.\\n\\n**Cluster Manager & Update Logic**: The cluster manager update logic is implemented in source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc/h, which is the central component coordinating cluster lifecycle. Supporting files include source/common/upstream/cluster_factory_impl.cc/h for cluster instantiation, source/common/upstream/cluster_update_tracker.cc/h for tracking updates, and source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc/h for core upstream functionality.\\n\\n**Active Health Checking**: The active health check infrastructure is built on source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.cc/h in the common layer. Protocol-specific health checker implementations are in source/extensions/health_checkers/: grpc/, http/, tcp/, redis/, and thrift/ subdirectories. Health check event logging is handled by source/common/upstream/health_checker_event_logger.cc/h. Health discovery service is implemented in source/common/upstream/health_discovery_service.cc/h. The scheduler integration for health checks is present in the base health checker implementation and scheduler classes in source/common/upstream/edf_scheduler.h and source/common/upstream/wrsq_scheduler.h.\\n\\n**Outlier Detection Integration**: Outlier detection is implemented in source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.cc/h, which integrates with the health checking and load balancing systems to handle host ejection based on abnormal behavior.\\n\\n**xDS Subscription & Configuration Management**: The gRPC subscription infrastructure for receiving cluster configuration updates is in source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/: grpc_subscription_impl.cc/h, grpc_mux_impl.cc/h, new_grpc_mux_impl.cc/h for multiplexed subscriptions, delta_subscription_state.cc/h for delta subscription logic, and xds_mux/ subdirectory for XDS-specific mux implementations. Supporting components include watch_map.cc/h for resource tracking, pausable_ack_queue.cc/h for ACK handling, and eds_resources_cache_impl.cc/h for endpoint resource caching.\\n\\n**Cluster Implementations**: Various cluster types that integrate with discovery include source/extensions/clusters/eds/ for endpoint discovery service clusters, source/extensions/clusters/aggregate/ for aggregated clusters, and source/extensions/clusters/ subdirectories for other cluster types like logical_dns, strict_dns, static, original_dst, and dynamic_forward_proxy.\\n\\n**Load Balancing Integration**: Load balancing policies in source/extensions/load_balancing_policies/ integrate with cluster health information and outlier detection. Key implementations include load_balancer_impl.cc/h and thread_aware_lb_impl.cc/h for the common framework, plus specific policies in round_robin/, least_request/, ring_hash/, maglev/, subset/, and random/ subdirectories.\\n\\n**Monitoring & Statistics**: Load statistics reporting for LDS (Load Distribution Service) is in source/common/upstream/load_stats_reporter.cc/h. components:\\n\\n**CDS (Cluster Discovery Service) Subscription**: The core CDS implementation resides in source/common/upstream/cds_api_impl.cc/h, which handles subscription to cluster discovery service. Additional CDS-related files include source/common/upstream/cds_api_helper.cc/h for helper utilities, source/common/upstream/cluster_discovery_manager.cc/h for managing cluster discovery, and source/common/upstream/od_cds_api_impl.cc/h for On-Demand CDS implementation.\\n\\n**Cluster Manager & Update Logic**: The cluster manager update logic is implemented in source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc/h, which is the central component coordinating cluster lifecycle. Supporting files include source/common/upstream/cluster_factory_impl.cc/h for cluster instantiation, source/common/upstream/cluster_update_tracker.cc/h for tracking updates, and source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc/h for core upstream functionality.\\n\\n**Active Health Checking**: The active health check infrastructure is built on source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.cc/h in the common layer. Protocol-specific health checker implementations are in source/extensions/health_checkers/: grpc/, http/, tcp/, redis/, and thrift/ subdirectories. Health check event logging is handled by source/common/upstream/health_checker_event_logger.cc/h. Health discovery service is implemented in source/common/upstream/health_discovery_service.cc/h. The scheduler integration for health checks is present in the base health checker implementation and scheduler classes in source/common/upstream/edf_scheduler.h and source/common/upstream/wrsq_scheduler.h.\\n\\n**Outlier Detection Integration**: Outlier detection is implemented in source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.cc/h, which integrates with the health checking and load balancing systems to handle host ejection based on abnormal behavior.\\n\\n**xDS Subscription & Configuration Management**: The gRPC subscription infrastructure for receiving cluster configuration updates is in source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/: grpc_subscription_impl.cc/h, grpc_mux_impl.cc/h, new_grpc_mux_impl.cc/h for multiplexed subscriptions, delta_subscription_state.cc/h for delta subscription logic, and xds_mux/ subdirectory for XDS-specific mux implementations. Supporting components include watch_map.cc/h for resource tracking, pausable_ack_queue.cc/h for ACK handling, and eds_resources_cache_impl.cc/h for endpoint resource caching.\\n\\n**Cluster Implementations**: Various cluster types that integrate with discovery include source/extensions/clusters/eds/ for endpoint discovery service clusters, source/extensions/clusters/aggregate/ for aggregated clusters, and source/extensions/clusters/ subdirectories for other cluster types like logical_dns, strict_dns, static, original_dst, and dynamic_forward_proxy.\\n\\n**Load Balancing Integration**: Load balancing policies in source/extensions/load_balancing_policies/ integrate with cluster health information and outlier detection. Key implementations include load_balancer_impl.cc/h and thread_aware_lb_impl.cc/h for the common framework, plus specific policies in round_robin/, least_request/, ring_hash/, maglev/, subset/, and random/ subdirectories.\\n\\n**Monitoring & Statistics**: Load statistics reporting for LDS (Load Distribution Service) is in source/common/upstream/load_stats_reporter.cc/h. Host utility functions for managing endpoint information are in source/common/upstream/host_utility.cc/h.\"\n   109→}\n   110→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. \"The Envoy codebase implements dynamic cluster discovery and health checking through several key components:\\n\\n**CDS (Cluster Discovery Service) Subscription**: The core CDS implementation resides in source/common/upstream/cds_api_impl.cc/h, which handles subscription to cluster discovery service. Additional CDS-related files include source/common/upstream/cds_api_helper.cc/h for helper utilities, source/common/upstream/cluster_discovery_manager.cc/h for managing cluster discovery, and source/common/upstream/od_cds_api_impl.cc/h for On-Demand CDS implementation.\\n\\n**Cluster Manager & Update Logic**: The cluster manager update logic is implemented in source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc/h, which is the central component coordinating cluster lifecycle. Supporting files include source/common/upstream/cluster_factory_impl.cc/h for cluster instantiation, source/common/upstream/cluster_update_tracker.cc/h for tracking updates, and source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc/h for core upstream functionality.\\n\\n**Active Health Checking**: The active health check infrastructure is built on source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.cc/h in the common layer. Protocol-specific health checker implementations are in source/extensions/health_checkers/: grpc/, http/, tcp/, redis/, and thrift/ subdirectories. Health check event logging is handled by source/common/upstream/health_checker_event_logger.cc/h. Health discovery service is implemented in source/common/upstream/health_discovery_service.cc/h. The scheduler integration for health checks is present in the base health checker implementation and scheduler classes in source/common/upstream/edf_scheduler.h and source/common/upstream/wrsq_scheduler.h.\\n\\n**Outlier Detection Integration**: Outlier detection is implemented in source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.cc/h, which integrates with the health checking and load balancing systems to handle host ejection based on abnormal behavior.\\n\\n**xDS Subscription & Configuration Management**: The gRPC subscription infrastructure for receiving cluster configuration updates is in source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/: grpc_subscription_impl.cc/h, grpc_mux_impl.cc/h, new_grpc_mux_impl.cc/h for multiplexed subscriptions, delta_subscription_state.cc/h for delta subscription logic, and xds_mux/ subdirectory for XDS-specific mux implementations. Supporting components include watch_map.cc/h for resource tracking, pausable_ack_queue.cc/h for ACK handling, and eds_resources_cache_impl.cc/h for endpoint resource caching.\\n\\n**Cluster Implementations**: Various cluster types that integrate with discovery include source/extensions/clusters/eds/ for endpoint discovery service clusters, source/extensions/clusters/aggregate/ for aggregated clusters, and source/extensions/clusters/ subdirectories for other cluster types like logical_dns, strict_dns, static, original_dst, and dynamic_forward_proxy.\\n\\n**Load Balancing Integration**: Load balancing policies in source/extensions/load_balancing_policies/ integrate with cluster health information and outlier detection. Key implementations include load_balancer_impl.cc/h and thread_aware_lb_impl.cc/h for the common framework, plus specific policies in round_robin/, least_request/, ring_hash/, maglev/, subset/, and random/ subdirectories.\\n\\n**Monitoring & Statistics**: Load statistics reporting for LDS (Load Distribution Service) is in source/common/upstream/load_stats_reporter.cc/h. Host utility functions for managing endpoint information are in source/common/upstream/host_utility.cc/h.\"\n}\n","numLines":110,"startLine":1,"totalLines":110}}}

\"The Envoy codebase implements dynamic cluster discovery and health checking through several key components:\\n\\n**CDS (Cluster Discovery Service) Subscription**: The core CDS implementation resides in source/common/upstream/cds_api_impl.cc/h, which handles subscription to cluster discovery service. Additional CDS-related files include source/common/upstream/cds_api_helper.cc/h for helper utilities, source/common/upstream/cluster_discovery_manager.cc/h for managing cluster discovery, and source/common/upstream/od_cds_api_impl.cc/h for On-Demand CDS implementation.\\n\\n**Cluster Manager & Update Logic**: The cluster manager update logic is implemented in source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc/h, which is the central component coordinating cluster lifecycle. Supporting files include source/common/upstream/cluster_factory_impl.cc/h for cluster instantiation, source/common/upstream/cluster_update_tracker.cc/h for tracking updates, and source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc/h for core upstream functionality.\\n\\n**Active Health Checking**: The active health check infrastructure is built on source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.cc/h in the common layer. Protocol-specific health checker implementations are in source/extensions/health_checkers/: grpc/, http/, tcp/, redis/, and thrift/ subdirectories. Health check event logging is handled by source/common/upstream/health_checker_event_logger.cc/h. Health discovery service is implemented in source/common/upstream/health_discovery_service.cc/h.
